          (conv_dir): Conv2d(384, 8, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
        )
      )
    )
    (rpn_acc): Accuracy()
    (rpn_precision): Precision()
    (rpn_recall): Recall()
    (rpn_metrics): PrecisionRecall()
    (rpn_cls_loss): Scalar()
    (rpn_loc_loss): Scalar()
    (rpn_total_loss): Scalar()
  )
)
